204)&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;Balance, December 31, 2018&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: Black 2.5pt double; text-align: left&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: Black 2.5pt double; text-align: right&gt;390,000&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: Black 2.5pt double; text-align: left&gt;$&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: Black 2.5pt double; text-align: right&gt;0.01&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: White&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: rgb(204
255
&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Note 16 - BRAC Rights&#13;and Warrants&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;i&gt;Initial Public Offering&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;i&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;Pursuant to the its Initial Public Offering&#13;and including the subsequent over-allotment option exercised by the underwriter, BRAC sold 13,800,000 Units at a purchase price&#13;of $10.00 per Unit. Each Unit consists of one share of common stock, one right (&amp;#8220;Public Right&amp;#8221;) and one warrant (&amp;#8220;Public&#13;Warrant&amp;#8221;). Each Public Right will convert into one-tenth (1/10) of one share of common stock upon consummation of a Business&#13;Combination. Each Public Warrant entitles the holder to purchase one share of common stock at an exercise price of $11.50.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;i&gt;Private Placement&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;i&gt; &amp;#160;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;Simultaneous with the its Initial Public&#13;Offering and over-allotment option exercise, BROG purchased an aggregate of 445,000 Placement Units at a price of $10.00 per Unit&#13;(or an aggregate purchase price of $4,450,000). Each Placement Unit consists of one share of common stock (&amp;#8220;Placement Share&amp;#8221;),&#13;one right (&amp;#8220;Placement Right&amp;#8221;) and one warrant (each, a &amp;#8220;Placement Warrant&amp;#8221;) to purchase one share of the&#13;common stock at an exercise price of $11.50 per share. The proceeds from the Placement Units were added to the proceeds from the&#13;Initial Public Offering held in the Trust Account. If BRAC does not complete a Business Combination within the Combination Period,&#13;the proceeds of the sale of the Placement Units will be used to fund the redemption of the Public Shares (subject to the requirements&#13;of applicable law) and the Placement Rights and Placement Warrants will expire worthless.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Placement Units are identical to the&#13;Units sold in the Initial Public Offering except that the Placement Warrants (i) are not redeemable by BRAC and (ii) may be exercised&#13;for cash or on a cashless basis, so long as they are held by BROG or any of its permitted transferees. In addition, the Placement&#13;Units and their component securities may not be transferable, assignable or salable until after the consummation of a Business&#13;Combination, subject to certain limited exceptions.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in&gt;&lt;i&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in&gt;&lt;i&gt;Rights&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in&gt;&lt;i&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;Each holder of a right will receive one-tenth&#13;(1/10) of one share of common stock upon consummation of a Business Combination, even if a holder of such right converted all ordinary&#13;shares held by it in connection with a Business Combination. No fractional shares will be issued upon exchange of the rights. No&#13;additional consideration will be required to be paid by a holder of rights in order to receive its additional shares upon consummation&#13;of a Business Combination as the consideration related thereto has been included in the Unit purchase price paid for by investors&#13;in the Initial Public Offering. If BRAC enters into a definitive agreement for a Business Combination in which BRAC will not be&#13;the surviving entity, the definitive agreement will provide for the holders of rights to receive the same per share consideration&#13;the holders of the shares of common stock will receive in the transaction on an as-converted into shares of common stock basis&#13;and each holder of rights will be required to affirmatively covert its rights in order to receive 1/10 of a share of common stock&#13;underlying each right (without paying additional consideration). The shares of common stock issuable upon exchange of the rights&#13;will be freely tradable (except to the extent held by affiliates of BRAC).&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;If BRAC is unable to complete a Business&#13;Combination within the Combination Period and BRAC liquidates the funds held in the Trust Account, holders of rights will not receive&#13;any of such funds with respect to their rights, nor will they receive any distribution from BRAC&amp;#8217;s assets held outside of&#13;the Trust Account with respect to such rights, and the rights will expire worthless. Further, there are no contractual penalties&#13;for failure to deliver securities to the holders of the rights upon consummation of a Business Combination. Additionally, in no&#13;event will BRAC be required to net cash settle the rights. Accordingly, the rights may expire worthless.&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;The rights included in the Private Units&#13;sold in the Private Placement are identical to the rights included in the Units sold in the Initial Public Offering, except that,&#13;among others, the rights including the shares issuable upon exchange of such rights, are being purchased pursuant to an exemption&#13;from the registration requirements of the Securities Act and will become tradable only after certain conditions are met or the&#13;resale of such rights (including underlying securities) is registered under the Securities Act.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;i&gt;Warrants&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;Warrants may only be exercised for a whole&#13;number of shares. No fractional shares will be issued upon exercise of the Warrants. The Warrants will become exercisable on the&#13;later of (a) 30 days after the consummation of a Business Combination or (b) October 10, 2018. No Warrants will be exercisable&#13;for cash unless BRAC has an effective and current registration statement covering the shares of common stock issuable upon exercise&#13;of the Warrants and a current prospectus relating to such shares. Notwithstanding the foregoing, if a registration statement covering&#13;the shares of common stock issuable upon the exercise of the Warrants is not effective within 30 days from the consummation of&#13;a Business Combination, the holders may, until such time as there is an effective registration statement and during any period&#13;when BRAC shall have failed to maintain an effective registration statement, exercise the Warrants on a cashless basis pursuant&#13;to an available exemption from registration under the Securities Act. If an exemption from registration is not available, holders&#13;will not be able to exercise their Warrants on a cashless basis. The Warrants will expire five years from the consummation of a&#13;Business Combination or earlier upon redemption or liquidation.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Private Warrants will be identical&#13;to the Warrants underlying the Units sold in the Initial Public Offering, except the Private Warrants will be exercisable for cash&#13;(even if a registration statement covering the shares of common stock issuable upon exercise of such Private Warrants is not effective)&#13;or on a cashless basis, at the holder&amp;#8217;s option, and will not be redeemable by BRAC, in each case so long as they are still&#13;held by BROG or its affiliates.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;BRAC may call the Warrants for redemption&#13;(excluding the Private Warrants but including any outstanding Warrants issued upon exercise of the unit purchase option issued&#13;to EarlyBirdCapital), in whole and not in part, at a price of $.01 per Warrant:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 style=width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt&gt;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;&lt;td style=width: 0.5in&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td style=width: 0.5in&gt;&lt;font style=font-family: Symbol&gt;&amp;#183;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;at any time while the Warrants are exercisable,&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 style=width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt&gt;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;&lt;td style=width: 0.5in&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td style=width: 0.5in&gt;&lt;font style=font-family: Symbol&gt;&amp;#183;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;upon not less than 30 days&amp;#8217; prior written notice of redemption to each Warrant holder,&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 style=width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt&gt;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;&lt;td style=width: 0.5in&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td style=width: 0.5in&gt;&lt;font style=font-family: Symbol&gt;&amp;#183;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;if, and only if, the reported last sale price of the shares of common stock equals or exceeds $18.00&#13;per share, for any 20 trading days within a 30 trading day period ending on the third business day prior to the notice of redemption&#13;to Warrant holders, and&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 style=width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt&gt;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;&lt;td style=width: 0.5in&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td style=width: 0.5in&gt;&lt;font style=font-family: Symbol&gt;&amp;#183;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;if, and only if, there is a current registration statement in effect with respect to the shares&#13;of common stock underlying such Warrants at the time of redemption and for the entire 30-day redemption period and continuing each&#13;day thereafter until the date of redemption.&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;If BRAC calls the Warrants for redemption,&#13;management will have the option to require all holders that wish to exercise the Warrants to do so on a &amp;#8220;cashless basis,&amp;#8221;&#13;as described in the warrant agreement.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;The exercise price and number of shares&#13;of common stock issuable upon exercise of the Warrants may be adjusted in certain circumstances including in the event of a stock&#13;dividend, extraordinary dividend or recapitalization, reorganization, merger or consolidation. However, the Warrants will not be&#13;adjusted for issuances of shares of common stock at a price below its exercise price. Additionally, in no event will BRAC be required&#13;to net cash settle the Warrants. If BRAC is unable to complete a Business Combination within the Combination Period and BRAC liquidates&#13;the funds held in the Trust Account, holders of Warrants will not receive any of such funds with respect to their Warrants, nor&#13;will they receive any distribution from BRAC&amp;#8217;s assets held outside of the Trust Account with respect to such Warrants. Accordingly,&#13;the Warrants may expire worthless.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;i&gt;Unit Purchase Option&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;The effective income tax rate for the years&#13;ended December&amp;#160;31,&amp;#160;2018 and 2017 consisted of the following:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Note 17 &amp;#8211; Income&#13;Taxes&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;We account for income taxes under the provisions&#13;of ASC Topic 740, &lt;i&gt;Income taxes, &lt;/i&gt;which provides for an asset and liability approach for income taxes. Under this approach,&#13;deferred tax assets and liabilities are recognized based on anticipated future tax consequences, using currently enacted tax laws,&#13;attributable to temporary differences between the carrying amounts of assets and liabilities for financial reporting purposes and&#13;the amounts calculated for income tax purposes.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Company will not consolidate income&#13;tax returns for Black Ridge Oil &amp;#38; Gas, Inc. and Black Ridge Acquisition Corp. For the years ended December 31, 2018 the impact&#13;of both returns are combined in the presentation.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;The 2018 and 2017 combined reconciliations&#13;above are weighted averages of the two separate taxable entities as such we have presented the individual entity reconciliations.&#13;When one entity has a loss and the other has income, the weighted average produces results that are skewed higher or lower than&#13;the individual components. BROG's state income tax rate as of December 31, 2018 increased by 4.1% from 3.6% as of December 31,&#13;2017, to 7.7%. This increase in the effective tax rate is attributable to changes in the federal rate. BRAC's state income tax&#13;rate as of December 31, 2018 increased by 0.9% from 6.8% as of December 31, 2017, to 7.7%.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

204)&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: White&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left&gt;Net deferred tax assets (liabilities)&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;9,735,333&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;8,712,615&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: rgb(204

204)&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left; text-indent: 13.5pt; padding-bottom: 1pt&gt;Less: valuation allowance&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid&gt;(9,735,771&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left; padding-bottom: 1pt&gt;)&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid&gt;(8,693,937&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left; padding-bottom: 1pt&gt;)&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: White&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left; padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;Deferred tax assets (liabilities)&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left; border-bottom: Black 2.5pt double&gt;$&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right; border-bottom: Black 2.5pt double&gt;(438&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left; padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;)&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left; border-bottom: Black 2.5pt double&gt;$&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right; border-bottom: Black 2.5pt double&gt;18,678&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: left; padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;As of December&amp;#160;31, 2018, the&#13;Company has net operating loss carryover of approximately $25,754,131. Under existing Federal law, the net operating loss may be&#13;utilized to offset taxable income through the year ended December&amp;#160;31, 2035. A portion of the net operating loss carryover&#13;begins to expire in 2030.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;ASC Topic 740 provides that a valuation&#13;allowance is recognized if, based on the weight of available evidence, it is more likely than not that some portion or all of the&#13;deferred tax asset will not be realized. In 2018, BROG increased its valuation allowance from $8,693,937 to $9,735,771 to adjust&#13;for the increase in net deferred tax assets primarily increased federal operating loss carryovers. The Company believes it is more&#13;likely than not that the benefit of these remaining assets will not be realized by BROG. The company did not place a valuation&#13;allowance on deferred tax asset for BRAC related to the capitalized merger and acquisition costs. The Company believes it is more&#13;likely than not that the benefit of these remaining assets will be realized by BRAC.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in&gt;The Company files annual&#13;US Federal income tax returns and annual income tax returns for the states of Minnesota, North Dakota and Montana. We are not subject&#13;to income tax examinations by tax authorities for years before 2013 for all returns. Income taxing authorities have conducted no&#13;formal examinations of our past federal or state income tax returns and supporting records.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in&gt;&lt;b&gt;Note 18 &amp;#8211; Commitments&#13;and Contingencies&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Company is involved in various inquiries,&#13;administrative proceedings and litigation relating to matters arising in the normal course of business. The Company is not currently&#13;a defendant in any material litigation and is not aware of any threatened litigation that could have a material effect on the Company.&#13;Management is not able to estimate the minimum loss to be incurred, if any, as a result of the final outcome of the matters arising&#13;in the normal course of business but believes they are not likely to have a material adverse effect upon the Company&amp;#8217;s financial&#13;position or results of operations and, accordingly, no provision for loss has been recorded.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Company periodically maintains cash&#13;balances at banks in excess of federally insured amounts. The extent of loss, if any, to be sustained as a result of any future&#13;failure of a bank or other financial institution is not subject to estimation at this time.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;i&gt;BRAC&amp;#8217;s agreements with underwriters&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;BRAC engaged the underwriters as advisors&#13;in connection with its Initial Business Combination to assist it in holding meetings with its shareholders to discuss the potential&#13;business combination and the target business&amp;#8217; attributes, introduce it to potential investors that are interested in purchasing&#13;its securities, assist it in obtaining shareholder approval for the business combination and assist it with its press releases&#13;and public filings in connection with the business combination. BRAC will pay its underwriters a cash fee for such services upon&#13;the consummation of its initial business combination in an amount equal to 3.5% of the gross proceeds of its offering (exclusive&#13;of any applicable finders&amp;#8217; fees which might become payable).&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Note 19 &amp;#8211; BRAC&amp;#8217;s Proposed&#13;Business Combination&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0&gt;&lt;i&gt;Business Combination Agreement&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;On December 19, 2018, BRAC entered into an Agreement and Plan&#13;of Reorganization (the &amp;#8220;Agreement&amp;#8221;) by and among BRAC, Black Ridge Merger Sub, Corp., a Delaware corporation and wholly-owned&#13;subsidiary of BRAC formed on December 19, 2018 (&amp;#8220;Merger Sub&amp;#8221;), Allied Esports Entertainment, Inc. (the &amp;#8220;Allied&#13;Esports&amp;#8221;), Ourgame International Holdings Ltd. (&amp;#8220;Ourgame&amp;#8221;), Noble Link Global Limited, a wholly-owned subsidiary&#13;of Ourgame (&amp;#8220;Noble&amp;#8221;), and Primo Vital Ltd., also a wholly-owned subsidiary of Ourgame (&amp;#8220;Primo&amp;#8221;).&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;Subject to the Agreement, (i) Noble will merge with and into&#13;Allied Esports (the &amp;#8220;Redomestication Merger&amp;#8221;) with Allied Esports being the surviving entity in such merger and (ii)&#13;immediately after the Redomestication Merger, Merger Sub will merge with and into Allied Esports with Allied Esports being the&#13;surviving entity of such merger (the &amp;#8220;Transaction Merger&amp;#8221; and together with the Redomestication Merger, the &amp;#8220;Mergers&amp;#8221;).&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Mergers will result in BRAC acquiring two of Ourgame&amp;#8217;s&#13;global esports and entertainment assets, Allied Esports International, Inc. (&amp;#8220;Allied Esports&amp;#8221;) and WPT Enterprises,&#13;Inc. (&amp;#8220;WPT&amp;#8221;). Allied Esports is a premier esports entertainment company with a global network of dedicated esports&#13;properties and content production facilities. WPT is the creator of the World Poker Tour&amp;#174; (WPT&amp;#174;) &amp;#8211; the premier name&#13;in internationally televised gaming and entertainment with brand presence in land-based tournaments, television, online and mobile.&#13;The proposed transaction will seek to strategically combine the globally recognized Allied Esports brand with the three-pronged&#13;business model of the iconic World Poker Tour, featuring in-person experiences, multiplatform content and interactive services,&#13;to leverage the high-growth opportunities in the global esports industry.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0&gt;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;Upon consummation of the Mergers (the &amp;#8220;Closing&amp;#8221;),&#13;BRAC will issue to the former owners of Allied Esports and WPT (i) an aggregate of 11,602,754 shares of common stock, par value&#13;$0.0001 per share, of BRAC&amp;#8217;s common stock and (ii) an aggregate of 3,800,003 warrants to purchase shares of common stock&#13;of BRAC.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;In addition to the consideration described above, the former&#13;owners of Allied Esports and WPT will be entitled to receive their pro rata portion of an aggregate of an additional 3,846,153&#13;shares of BRAC&amp;#8217;s common stock if the last sales price of BRAC&amp;#8217;s common stock equals or exceeds $13.00 per share (as&#13;adjusted for stock splits, stock dividends, reorganizations and recapitalizations) for thirty (30) consecutive days at any time&#13;during the five (5) year period commencing on the date of the Closing (the &amp;#8220;Closing Date&amp;#8221;).&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;i&gt;Proposed Changes to the Capital Structure&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;i&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;BRAC is seeking shareholder approval to&#13;amend its charter to increase the authorized shares of BRAC&amp;#8217;s common stock to 65,000,000 shares.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;i&gt;Conditions to Consummation of the Business&#13;Combination&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;i&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify&gt;Consummation of the transactions contemplated by the Agreement&#13;is subject to certain closing conditions including, among others, (i) approval by the stockholders of BRAC and Ourgame, and (ii)&#13;that BRAC have available cash in an amount not less than $80,000,000 after payment to stockholders who elect to redeem their shares&#13;of common stock in accordance with the provisions of BRAC&amp;#8217;s Charter Documents.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
